province_event = {
	id = 999968
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.2
	  NOT = { literacy = 0.3 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_2 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
			remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_1
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_3

            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_6

province_event = {
	id = 999967
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.3
	  NOT = { literacy = 0.4 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_3 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
			remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_1
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_2
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_4
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_5
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_6
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_7

province_event = {
	id = 999966
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.4
	  NOT = { literacy = 0.5 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_4 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
			remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_1
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_2
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_3
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_5
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_6
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_7

province_event = {
	id = 999965
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.5
	  NOT = { literacy = 0.6 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_5 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"

			any_owned = {

province_event = {
	id = 999964
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.6
	  NOT = { literacy = 0.7 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_6 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
			remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_1
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_2
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_3
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_4
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_5

province_event = {
	id = 999963
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.7
	  NOT = { literacy = 0.8 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_7 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"

			any_owned = {

province_event = {
	id = 999962
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.8
	  NOT = { literacy = 0.9 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_8 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
			remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_1
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_2

            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_4
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_5
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_6

province_event = {
	id = 999961
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0.9
	  NOT = { literacy = 1 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_9 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"

			any_owned = {

            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_2

            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_5

province_event = {
	id = 999960
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 1
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_10 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
			remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_1
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_2
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_3
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_4
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_5
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_6

province_event = {
	id = 999959
	title = "Education in $STATENAME$"
	desc = "Education in $STATENAME$ accelerates economic growth."

	trigger = {
	has_global_flag = education_setup
      state_scope = {
	  literacy = 0
      NOT = { literacy = 0.1 }
	  }
	  NOT = { has_province_modifier = RGO_education_0 }
	}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Advance $COUNTRY$ !"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
			remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_1
            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_2

            remove_province_modifier = RGO_education_5
